                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: লাল পিপঁড়া ও ভিমরুলের গ্ল্যান্ডে- ফরমিক এসিড; ভিনেগারে- অ্যাসিটিক এসিড; টকযুক্ত মাখন বা বাটারে- বিউটানোয়িক এসিড; পাম অয়েলে- পামিটিক এসিড।<br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২৩, পৃষ্ঠা-২৯৬]</p>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>

width: 0px; height: 2.279em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.219em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.169em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mn>90</mn><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mo>°</mo></mrow><mo>&lt;</mo><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mo>θ</mo></mrow><mo>≤</mo><mn>180</mn><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mo>°</mo></mrow></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-63">\rm 90°<θ≤180° </script></span></p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: &nbsp;বলের দ্বারা কাজের ক্ষেত্রে <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit;                                             </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">

                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>get</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>If বা in case দ্বারা যুক্ত একটি clause future tense- এ হলে অপর clause টি present indefinite tense- এ হবে। সুতরাং সঠিক verb form হলো get।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                                <span class="input-group-text">A</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>if you had had an opportunity</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">

                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>if you had an opportunity</p>

                                    </div>

                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>if you have had an opportunity</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">

                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>

                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Perfect conditional sentence অনুযায়ী If যুক্ত clause টি Past perfect tense এর হলে, main clause এর&nbsp;verb form might/should/would + have + v<sub>3</sub> (Past participle) অনুযায়ী অনুসৃত হবে।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                            <span>Question 86 </span>
                                        </div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>People always remember the patriots. Which of the following is the best passive form of the above sentence?</p>

                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>

                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">A</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>The patriots will always be remembered by people.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">B</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>The patriots are always being remembered.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>People are always remembered by the patriots.</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group" style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text" style="font-weight:bold;">D</span>
                                            </div>
                                            <div class="input-group-append questionTable">
                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>The patriots are always remembered.</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>বাক্যটি Present indefinite tense এ থাকায় এর passive রূপ হবে: Sub (obj) + be verb + adverb of time + verb- এর past participle + by + obj (sub)। তবে by + obj অংশটি উল্লেখ না করলেও বাক্য ভুল হয় না।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                                            </div>
                                        </div>

                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>ট্রেনটি ঢাকা যাবে-এর translation হলো The train is bound for Dhaka। Be bound for অর্থ কোনো স্থানে গমনরত বা ভবিষ্যত কোনো স্থানে গমনে প্রস্তুত।</p>
